Description:
ACCT 2301 - Introductory Financial Accounting (3 semester credit hours) An introduction to financial reporting designed to create an awareness of the accounting concepts and principles for preparing the three basic financial statements: the income statement, balance sheet, and statement of cash flows. A minimum grade of C is required to take upper-division ACCT courses. (3-0) S
